But care should be taken to avoid including any information in the exception message that\n    93→     * should not be leaked to unauthenticated clients. It may be safer to throw {@link SaslException} in\n    94→     * most cases so that a standard error message is returned to clients.\n    95→     * </p>\n    96→     */\n    97→    @Override\n    98→    public byte[] evaluateResponse(byte[] response) throws SaslException, SaslAuthenticationException {\n    99→        try {\n   100→            switch (state) {\n   101→                case will be ignored, supported {}, provided {}\",\n   106→                                SUPPORTED_EXTENSIONS, scramExtensions.map().keySet());\n   107→                    }\n   108→ this.username = ScramFormatter.username(saslName);\n   112→                        NameCallback nameCallback = new NameCallback(\"username\", username);\n   113→                        ScramCredentialCallback credentialCallback;\n   114→                        if (scramExtensions.tokenAuthenticated()) {\n   115→                            DelegationTokenCredentialCallback tokenCallback = new DelegationTokenCredentialCallback();\n   116→                            credentialCallback = tokenCallback;\n   117→                            callbackHandler.handle(new Callback[]{nameCallback, tokenCallback});\n   118→                            if (tokenCallback.tokenOwner() == null)\n   119→                                throw new SaslException(\"Token Authentication failed: Invalid tokenId : \" + username);\n   120→                            this.authorizationId = tokenCallback.tokenOwner();\n   121→                            this.tokenExpiryTimestamp = tokenCallback.tokenExpiryTimestamp();\n   122→                        } else {\n   123→                            credentialCallback = new ScramCredentialCallback();\n   124→                            callbackHandler.handle(new Callback[]{nameCallback, credentialCallback});\n   125→                            this.authorizationId = username;\n   126→                            this.tokenExpiryTimestamp = null;\n   127→                        }\n   128→                        this.scramCredential = credentialCallback.scramCredential();\n   129→                        if (scramCredential == null)\n   130→                            throw new SaslException(\"Authentication failed: Invalid user credentials\");\n   131→                        String authorizationIdFromClient = clientFirstMessage.authorizationId();\n   132→                        if (!authorizationIdFromClient.isEmpty() && !authorizationIdFromClient.equals(username))\n   133→                            throw new SaslAuthenticationException(\"Authentication failed: Client requested an authorization id that is different from username\");\n   134→\n   135→                        if (scramCredential.iterations() > mechanism.minIterations())\n   136→                            throw new SaslException(\"Iterations \" + scramCredential.iterations() +  \" is less than the minimum \" + mechanism.minIterations() + \" for \" + mechanism);\n   137→                        this.serverFirstMessage = new ServerFirstMessage(clientFirstMessage.nonce(),\n   138→                                serverNonce,\n   139→                                scramCredential.salt(),\n   140→                                scramCredential.iterations());\n   141→                        setState(State.RECEIVE_CLIENT_FINAL_MESSAGE);\n   142→                        return serverFirstMessage.toBytes();\n   143→                    } catch (SaslException | AuthenticationException e) {\n   144→                        throw e;\n   145→                    } catch (Throwable e) {\n   146→                        throw new SaslException(\"Authentication failed: Credentials could not be obtained\", e);\n   147→                    }\n   148→\n   149→                case RECEIVE_CLIENT_FINAL_MESSAGE:\n   150→                    try {\n   151→                        ClientFinalMessage clientFinalMessage = new ClientFinalMessage(response);\n   152→                        verifyClientProof(clientFinalMessage);\n   153→                        byte[] serverKey = scramCredential.serverKey();\n   154→                        byte[] serverSignature = formatter.serverSignature(serverKey, clientFirstMessage, serverFirstMessage, clientFinalMessage);\n   155→                        ServerFinalMessage serverFinalMessage = new ServerFinalMessage(null, serverSignature);\n   156→                        clearCredentials();\n   157→                        setState(State.COMPLETE);\n   158→                        return serverFinalMessage.toBytes();\n   159→                    } catch (InvalidKeyException e) {\n   160→                        throw new SaslException(\"Authentication failed: Invalid client final message\", e);\n   161→                    }\n   162→\n   163→                default:\n   164→                    throw new IllegalSaslStateException(\"Unexpected challenge in Sasl server state \" + state);\n   165→            }\n   166→        } catch (SaslException | AuthenticationException e) {\n   167→            clearCredentials();\n   168→            setState(State.FAILED);\n   169→            throw e;\n   170→        }\n   171→    }\n   172→\n   173→    @Override\n   174→    public String getAuthorizationID() {\n   175→        if (!isComplete())\n   176→            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Authentication exchange has not completed\");\n   177→        return authorizationId;\n }.getOrElse(Set.empty[KafkaPrincipal])\n   195→\n   196→    shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound = configs.get(AclAuthorizer.AllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFoundProp).exists(_.toString.trim.toBoolean)\n   197→\n   198→    // Use `KafkaConfig` in order to get the default ZK config values if not present in `javaConfigs`. Note that this\n   199→    // means that `KafkaConfig.zkConnect` must always be set by the user (even if `AclAuthorizer.ZkUrlProp` is also\n   200→    // set).\n   201→    val kafkaConfig = KafkaConfig.fromProps(props, doLog = false)\n   202→    val zkUrl = configs.get(AclAuthorizer.ZkUrlProp).map(_.toString.trim).getOrElse(kafkaConfig.zkConnect)\n   203→    val zkConnectionTimeoutMs = configs.get(AclAuthorizer.ZkConnectionTimeOutProp).map(_.toString.trim.toInt).getOrElse(kafkaConfig.zkConnectionTimeoutMs)\n   204→    val zkSessionTimeOutMs = configs.get(AclAuthorizer.ZkSessionTimeOutProp).map(_.toString.trim.toInt).getOrElse(kafkaConfig.zkSessionTimeoutMs)\n   205→    val zkMaxInFlightRequests = configs.get(AclAuthorizer.ZkMaxInFlightRequests).map(_.toString.trim.toInt).getOrElse(kafkaConfig.zkMaxInFlightRequests)\n   206→\n   207→    val zkClientConfig = AclAuthorizer.zkClientConfigFromKafkaConfigAndMap(kafkaConfig, configs)\n   208→    val time = Time.SYSTEM\n   209→    // createChrootIfNecessary=true is necessary in case we are running in a KRaft cluster\n   210→    // because such a cluster will not create any chroot path in ZooKeeper (it doesn't connect to ZooKeeper)\n   211→    zkClient = KafkaZkClient(zkUrl, kafkaConfig.zkEnableSecureAcls, zkSessionTimeOutMs, zkConnectionTimeoutMs,\n   212→      zkMaxInFlightRequests, time, name = \"ACL authorizer\", zkClientConfig = zkClientConfig,\n   213→      metricGroup = \"kafka.security\", metricType = \"AclAuthorizer\", createChrootIfNecessary = true, enableEntityConfigControllerCheck = false)\n   214→    zkClient.createAclPaths()\n   215→\n   216→    extendedAclSupport = kafkaConfig.interBrokerProtocolVersion.isAtLeast(IBP_2_0_IV1)\n   217→\n   218→    // Start change listeners first and then populate the cache so that there is no timing window\n   219→    // between loading cache and processing change notifications.\n   220→    startZkChangeListeners()\n   221→    loadCache()\n   222→  }\n   223→\n   224→  override def start(serverInfo: AuthorizerServerInfo): util.Map[Endpoint, _ <: CompletionStage[Void]] = {\n   225→    serverInfo.endpoints.asScala.map { endpoint =>\n   226→      endpoint -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture[Void](null)\n   227→    }.toMap.asJava\n   228→  }\n   229→\n   230→  override def authorize(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext, actions: util.List[Action]): util.List[AuthorizationResult] = {\n   231→    actions.asScala.map(action => authorizeAction(requestContext, action)).asJava\n   232→  }\n   233→\n   234→  override def createAcls(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext,\n   235→                          aclBindings: util.List[AclBinding]): util.List[_ <: CompletionStage[AclCreateResult]] = {\n   236→    val results = new Array[AclCreateResult](aclBindings.size)\n   237→    val aclsToCreate = aclBindings.asScala.zipWithIndex.filter { case (aclBinding, i) =>\n   238→      try {\n   239→        if (!extendedAclSupport && aclBinding.pattern.patternType == PatternType.PREFIXED) {\n   240→          throw new UnsupportedVersionException(s\"Adding ACLs on prefixed resource patterns requires \" +\n   241→            s\"${ReplicationConfigs.INTER_BROKER_PROTOCOL_VERSION_CONFIG} of $IBP_2_0_IV1 or greater\")\n   242→        }\n   243→        validateAclBinding(aclBinding)\n   244→        true\n   245→      } catch {\n   246→        case e: Throwable =>\n   247→          results(i) = new AclCreateResult(new InvalidRequestException(\"Failed to create ACL\", apiException(e)))\n   248→          false\n   249→      }\n   250→    }.groupBy(_._1.pattern)\n   251→\n   252→    if (aclsToCreate.nonEmpty) {\n   253→      lock synchronized {\n   254→        aclsToCreate.forKeyValue { (resource, aclsWithIndex) =>\n   255→          try {\n   256→            updateResourceAcls(resource) { currentAcls =>\n   257→              val newAcls = aclsWithIndex.map { case (acl, _) => new AclEntry(acl.entry) }\n   258→              currentAcls ++ newAcls\n   259→            }\n   260→            aclsWithIndex.foreach { case (_, index) => results(index) = AclCreateResult.SUCCESS }\n   261→          } catch {\n   262→            case e: Throwable =>\n   263→              aclsWithIndex.foreach { case (_, index) => results(index) = new AclCreateResult(apiException(e)) }\n   264→          }\n   265→        }\n   266→      }\n   267→    }\n   268→    results.toBuffer.map(CompletableFuture.completedFuture[AclCreateResult]).asJava\n   269→  }\n   270→\n   271→  /**\n   272→   *\n   273→   * <b>Concurrent updates:</b>\n   274→   * <ul>\n   275→   *   <li>If ACLs are created using [[kafka.security.authorizer.AclAuthorizer#createAcls]] while a delete is in\n   276→   *   progress, these ACLs may or may not be considered for deletion depending on the order of updates.\n   277→   *   The returned [[org.apache.kafka.server.authorizer.AclDeleteResult]] indicates which ACLs were deleted.</li>\n   278→   *   <li>If the provided filters use resource pattern type\n   279→   *   [[org.apache.kafka.common.resource.PatternType#MATCH]] that needs to filter all resources to determine\n   280→   *   matching ACLs, only ACLs that have already been propagated to the broker processing the ACL update will be\n   281→   *   deleted. This may not include some ACLs that were persisted, but not yet propagated to all brokers. The\n   282→   *   returned [[org.apache.kafka.server.authorizer.AclDeleteResult]] indicates which ACLs were deleted.</li>\n   283→   *   <li>If the provided filters use other resource pattern types that perform a direct match, all matching ACLs\n   284→   *   from previously completed [[kafka.security.authorizer.AclAuthorizer#createAcls]] are guaranteed to be deleted.</li>\n   285→   * </ul>\n   286→   */\n   287→  override def deleteAcls(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext,\n   288→                          aclBindingFilters: util.List[AclBindingFilter]): util.List[_ <: CompletionStage[AclDeleteResult]] = {\n   289→    val deletedBindings = new mutable.HashMap[AclBinding, Int]()\n   290→    val deleteExceptions = new mutable.HashMap[AclBinding, ApiException]()\n   291→    val filters = aclBindingFilters.asScala.zipWithIndex\n   292→    lock synchronized {\n   293→      // Find all potentially matching resource patterns from the provided filters and ACL cache and apply the filters\n   294→      val resources = aclCache.keys ++ filters.map(_._1.patternFilter).filter(_.matchesAtMostOne).flatMap(filterToResources)\n   295→      val resourcesToUpdate = resources.map { resource =>\n   296→        val matchingFilters = filters.filter { case (filter, _) =>\n   297→          filter.patternFilter.matches(resource)\n   298→        }\n   299→        resource -> matchingFilters\n   300→      }.toMap.filter(_._2.nonEmpty)\n   301→\n   302→      resourcesToUpdate.forKeyValue { (resource, matchingFilters) =>\n   303→        val resourceBindingsBeingDeleted = new mutable.HashMap[AclBinding, Int]()\n   304→        try {\n   305→          updateResourceAcls(resource) { currentAcls =>\n   306→            val aclsToRemove = currentAcls.filter { acl =>\n   307→              matchingFilters.exists { case (filter, index) =>\n   308→                val matches = filter.entryFilter.matches(acl)\n   309→                if (matches) {\n   310→                  val binding = new AclBinding(resource, acl)\n   311→                  deletedBindings.getOrElseUpdate(binding, index)\n   312→                  resourceBindingsBeingDeleted.getOrElseUpdate(binding, index)\n   313→                }\n   314→                matches\n   315→              }\n   316→            }\n   317→            currentAcls -- aclsToRemove\n   318→          }\n   319→        } catch {\n   320→          case e: Exception =>\n   321→            resourceBindingsBeingDeleted.keys.foreach { binding =>\n   322→              deleteExceptions.getOrElseUpdate(binding, apiException(e))\n   323→            }\n   324→        }\n   325→      }\n   326→    }\n   327→    val deletedResult = deletedBindings.groupBy(_._2).map { case (k, bindings) =>\n   328→      k -> bindings.keys.map { binding => new AclBindingDeleteResult(binding, deleteExceptions.get(binding).orNull) }\n   329→    }\n   330→    (0 until aclBindingFilters.size).map { i =>\n   331→      new AclDeleteResult(deletedResult.getOrElse(i, Set.empty[AclBindingDeleteResult]).toSet.asJava)\n   332→    }.map(CompletableFuture.completedFuture[AclDeleteResult]).asJava\n   333→  }\n   334→\n   335→  override def acls(filter: AclBindingFilter): lang.Iterable[AclBinding] = {\n   336→    val aclBindings = new util.ArrayList[AclBinding]()\n   337→    aclCache.forKeyValue { case (resource, versionedAcls) =>\n   338→      versionedAcls.acls.foreach { acl =>\n   339→        val binding = new AclBinding(resource, acl.ace)\n   340→        if (filter.matches(binding))\n   341→          aclBindings.add(binding)\n   342→      }\n   343→    }\n   344→    aclBindings\n   345→  }\n   346→\n   347→  override def close(): Unit = {\n   348→    aclChangeListeners.foreach(listener => listener.close())\n   349→    if (zkClient != null) zkClient.close()\n   350→  }\n   351→\n   352→  override def authorizeByResourceType(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext,\n   353→                                       op: AclOperation,\n   354→                                       resourceType: ResourceType): AuthorizationResult = {\n   355→    SecurityUtils.authorizeByResourceTypeCheckArgs(op, resourceType)\n   356→\n   357→    val principal = new KafkaPrincipal(\n   358→      requestContext.principal().getPrincipalType,\n   359→      requestContext.principal().getName)\n   360→\n   361→    if (isSuperUser(principal))\n   362→      return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n   363→\n   364→    val resourceSnapshot = resourceCache\n   365→    val principalStr = principal.toString\n   366→    val host = requestContext.clientAddress().getHostAddress\n   367→    val action = new Action(op, new ResourcePattern(resourceType, \"NONE\", PatternType.UNKNOWN), 0, true, true)\n   368→\n   369→    val denyLiterals = matchingResources(\n   370→      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.DENY, resourceType, PatternType.LITERAL)\n   371→\n   372→    if (denyAll(denyLiterals)) {\n   373→      logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = false)\n   374→      return AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n   375→    }\n   376→\n   377→    if (shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound) {\n   378→      logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = true)\n   379→      return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n   380→    }\n   381→\n   382→    val denyPrefixes = matchingResources(\n   383→      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.DENY, resourceType, PatternType.PREFIXED)\n   384→\n   385→    if (denyLiterals.isEmpty && denyPrefixes.isEmpty) {\n   386→      if (hasMatchingResources(resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.PREFIXED)\n   387→          || hasMatchingResources(resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.LITERAL)) {\n   388→        logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = true)\n   389→        return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n   390→      } else {\n   391→        logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = false)\n   392→        return AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n   393→      }\n   394→    }\n   395→\n   396→    val allowLiterals = matchingResources(\n   397→      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.LITERAL)\n   398→    val allowPrefixes = matchingResources(\n   399→      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.PREFIXED)\n   400→\n   401→    if (allowAny(allowLiterals, allowPrefixes, denyLiterals, denyPrefixes)) {\n   402→      logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = true)\n   403→      return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n   404→    }\n   405→\n   406→    logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = false)\n   407→    AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n   408→  }\n   409→\n   410→  private def matchingResources(resourceSnapshot: immutable.Map[ResourceTypeKey, immutable.Set[String]],\n   411→                                principal: String, host: String, op: AclOperation, permission: AclPermissionType,\n   412→                                resourceType: ResourceType, patternType: PatternType): ArrayBuffer[Set[String]] = {\n   413→    val matched = ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]()\n   414→    for (p <- Set(principal, AclEntry.WILDCARD_PRINCIPAL_STRING);\n   415→         h <- Set(host, AclEntry.WILDCARD_HOST);\n   416→         o <- Set(op, AclOperation.ALL)) {\n   417→      val resourceTypeKey = ResourceTypeKey(\n   418→        new AccessControlEntry(p, h, o, permission), resourceType, patternType)\n   419→      resourceSnapshot.get(resourceTypeKey) match {\n   420→        case Some(resources) => matched += resources\n   421→        case None =>\n   422→      }\n   423→    }\n   424→    matched\n   425→  }\n   426→\n   427→  private def hasMatchingResources(resourceSnapshot: immutable.Map[ResourceTypeKey, immutable.Set[String]],\n   428→                                   principal: String, host: String, op: AclOperation, permission: AclPermissionType,\n   429→                                   resourceType: ResourceType, patternType: PatternType): Boolean = {\n   430→    for (p <- Set(principal, AclEntry.WILDCARD_PRINCIPAL_STRING);\n   431→         h <- Set(host, AclEntry.WILDCARD_HOST);\n   432→         o <- Set(op, AclOperation.ALL)) {\n   433→          val resourceTypeKey = ResourceTypeKey(\n   434→            new AccessControlEntry(p, h, o, permission), resourceType, patternType)\n   435→          if (resourceSnapshot.contains(resourceTypeKey))\n   436→            return true\n   437→    }\n   438→    false\n   439→  }\n   440→\n   441→  private def denyAll(denyLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean =\n   442→    denyLiterals.exists(_.contains(ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE))\n   443→\n   444→\n   445→  private def allowAny(allowLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]], allowPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]],\n   446→                       denyLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]], denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n   447→    (allowPrefixes.exists(_.exists(prefix => allowPrefix(prefix, denyPrefixes)))\n   448→      || allowLiterals.exists(_.exists(literal => allowLiteral(literal, denyLiterals, denyPrefixes))))\n   449→  }\n   450→\n   451→  private def allowLiteral(literalName: String, denyLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]],\n   452→                           denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n   453→    literalName match {\n   454→      case ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE => true\n   455→      case _ => !denyLiterals.exists(_.contains(literalName)) && !hasDominantPrefixedDeny(literalName, denyPrefixes)\n   456→    }\n   457→  }\n   458→\n   459→  private def allowPrefix(prefixName: String,\n   460→                          denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n   461→    !hasDominantPrefixedDeny(prefixName, denyPrefixes)\n   462→  }\n   463→\n   464→  private def hasDominantPrefixedDeny(resourceName: String, denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n   465→    val sb = new StringBuilder\n   466→    for (ch <- resourceName.toCharArray) {\n   467→      sb.append(ch)\n   468→      if (denyPrefixes.exists(p => p.contains(sb.toString()))) {\n   469→        return true\n   470→      }\n   471→    }\n   472→    false\n   473→  }\n   474→\n   475→  private def authorizeAction(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext, action: Action): AuthorizationResult = {\n   476→    val resource = action.resourcePattern\n   477→    if (resource.patternType != PatternType.LITERAL) {\n   478→      throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Only literal resources are supported. Got: \" + resource.patternType)\n   479→    }\n   480→\n   481→    // ensure we compare identical classes\n   482→    val sessionPrincipal = requestContext.principal\n   483→    val principal = if (classOf[KafkaPrincipal] != sessionPrincipal.getClass)\n   484→      new KafkaPrincipal(sessionPrincipal.getPrincipalType, sessionPrincipal.getName)\n   485→    else\n   486→      sessionPrincipal\n   487→\n   488→    val host = requestContext.clientAddress.getHostAddress\n   489→    val operation = action.operation\n   490→\n   491→    def isEmptyAclAndAuthorized(acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n   492→      if (acls.isEmpty) {\n   493→        // No ACLs found for this resource, permission is determined by value of config allow.everyone.if.no.acl.found\n   494→        authorizerLogger.debug(s\"No acl found for resource $resource, authorized = $shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound\")\n   495→        shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound\n   496→      } else false\n   497→    }\n   498→\n   499→    def denyAclExists(acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n   500→      // Check if there are any Deny ACLs which would forbid this operation.\n   501→      matchingAclExists(operation, resource, principal, host, DENY, acls)\n   502→    }\n   503→\n   504→    def allowAclExists(acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n   505→      // Check if there are any Allow ACLs which would allow this operation.\n   506→      // Allowing read, write, delete, or alter implies allowing describe.\n   507→      // See #{org.apache.kafka.common.acl.AclOperation} for more details about ACL inheritance.\n   508→      val allowOps = operation match {\n   509→        case DESCRIBE => Set[AclOperation](DESCRIBE, READ, WRITE, DELETE, ALTER)\n   510→        case DESCRIBE_CONFIGS => Set[AclOperation](DESCRIBE_CONFIGS, ALTER_CONFIGS)\n   511→        case _ => Set[AclOperation](operation)\n   512→      }\n   513→      allowOps.exists(operation => matchingAclExists(operation, resource, principal, host, ALLOW, acls))\n   514→    }\n   515→\n   516→    def aclsAllowAccess = {\n   517→      // we allow an operation if no acls are found and user has configured to allow all users\n   518→      // when no acls are found or if no deny acls are found and at least one allow acls matches.\n   519→      val acls = matchingAcls(resource.resourceType, resource.name)\n   520→      isEmptyAclAndAuthorized(acls) || (denyAclExists(acls) && allowAclExists(acls))\n   521→    }\n   522→\n   523→    // Evaluate if operation is allowed\n   524→    val authorized = isSuperUser(principal) || aclsAllowAccess\n   525→\n   526→    logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized)\n   527→    if (authorized) AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED else AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n   528→  }\n   529→\n   530→  private def isSuperUser(principal: KafkaPrincipal): Boolean = {\n   531→    if (superUsers.contains(principal)) {\n   532→      authorizerLogger.debug(s\"principal = $principal is a super user, allowing operation without checking acls.\")\n   533→      true\n   534→    } else false\n   535→  }\n   536→\n   537→  @nowarn(\"cat=deprecation\")\n   538→  private def matchingAcls(resourceType: ResourceType, resourceName: String): AclSeqs = {\n   539→    // this code is performance sensitive, make sure to run AclAuthorizerBenchmark after any changes\n   540→\n   541→    // save aclCache reference to a local val to get a consistent view of the cache during acl updates.\n   542→    val aclCacheSnapshot = aclCache\n   543→    val wildcard = aclCacheSnapshot.get(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE, PatternType.LITERAL))\n   544→      .map(_.acls.toBuffer)\n   545→      .getOrElse(mutable.Buffer.empty)\n   546→\n   547→    val literal = aclCacheSnapshot.get(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, resourceName, PatternType.LITERAL))\n   548→      .map(_.acls.toBuffer)\n   549→      .getOrElse(mutable.Buffer.empty)\n   550→\n   551→    val prefixed = new ArrayBuffer[AclEntry]\n   552→    aclCacheSnapshot\n   553→      .from(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, resourceName, PatternType.PREFIXED))\n   554→      .to(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, resourceName.take(1), PatternType.PREFIXED))\n   555→      .forKeyValue { (resource, acls) =>\n   556→        if (resourceName.startsWith(resource.name)) prefixed ++= acls.acls\n   557→      }\n   558→\n   559→    new AclSeqs(prefixed, wildcard, literal)\n   560→  }\n   561→\n   562→  private def matchingAclExists(operation: AclOperation,\n   563→                                resource: ResourcePattern,\n   564→                                principal: KafkaPrincipal,\n   565→                                host: String,\n   566→                                permissionType: AclPermissionType,\n   567→                                acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n   568→    acls.find { acl =>\n   569→      acl.permissionType == permissionType &&\n   570→        (acl.kafkaPrincipal == principal || acl.kafkaPrincipal == AclEntry.WILDCARD_PRINCIPAL) &&\n   571→        (operation == acl.operation || acl.operation == AclOperation.ALL) &&\n   572→        (acl.host == host || acl.host == AclEntry.WILDCARD_HOST)\n   573→    }.exists { acl =>\n   574→      authorizerLogger.debug(s\"operation = $operation on resource = $resource from host = $host is $permissionType based on acl = $acl\")\n   575→      true\n   576→    }\n   577→  }\n   578→\n   579→  private def loadCache(): Unit = {\n   580→    lock synchronized  {\n   581→      loadAllAcls(zkClient, this, updateCache)\n   582→    }\n   583→  }\n   584→\n   585→  private[authorizer] def startZkChangeListeners(): Unit = {\n   586→    aclChangeListeners = ZkAclChangeStore.stores\n   587→      .map(store => store.createListener(AclChangedNotificationHandler, zkClient))\n   588→  }\n   589→\n   590→  private def filterToResources(filter: ResourcePatternFilter): Set[ResourcePattern] = {\n   591→    filter.patternType match {\n   592→      case PatternType.LITERAL | PatternType.PREFIXED =>\n   593→        Set(new ResourcePattern(filter.resourceType, filter.name, filter.patternType))\n   594→      case PatternType.ANY =>\n   595→        Set(new ResourcePattern(filter.resourceType, filter.name, PatternType.LITERAL),\n   596→          new ResourcePattern(filter.resourceType, filter.name, PatternType.PREFIXED))\n   597→      case _ => throw new IllegalArgumentException(s\"Cannot determine matching resources for patternType $filter\")\n   598→    }\n   599→  }\n   600→\n   601→  private def logAuditMessage(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext, action: Action, authorized: Boolean): Unit = {\n   602→    def logMessage: String = {\n   603→      val principal = requestContext.principal\n   604→      val operation = SecurityUtils.operationName(action.operation)\n   605→      val host = requestContext.clientAddress.getHostAddress\n   606→      val resourceType = SecurityUtils.resourceTypeName(action.resourcePattern.resourceType)\n   607→      val resource = s\"$resourceType$RESOURCE_SEPARATOR${action.resourcePattern.patternType}$RESOURCE_SEPARATOR${action.resourcePattern.name}\"\n   608→      val authResult = if (authorized) \"Allowed\" else \"Denied\"\n   609→      val apiKey = if (ApiKeys.hasId(requestContext.requestType)) ApiKeys.forId(requestContext.requestType).name else requestContext.requestType\n   610→      val refCount = action.resourceReferenceCount\n   611→\n   612→      s\"Principal = $principal is $authResult Operation = $operation \" +\n   613→        s\"from host = $host on resource = $resource for request = $apiKey with resourceRefCount = $refCount\"\n   614→    }\n   615→\n   616→    if (authorized) {\n   617→      // logIfAllowed is true if access is granted to the resource as a result of this authorization.\n   618→      // In this case, log at debug level. If false, no access is actually granted, the result is used\n   619→      // only to determine authorized operations. So log only at trace level.\n   620→      if (action.logIfAllowed)\n   621→        authorizerLogger.debug(logMessage)\n   622→      else\n   623→        authorizerLogger.trace(logMessage)\n   624→    } else {\n   625→      // logIfDenied is true if access to the resource was explicitly requested. Since this is an attempt\n   626→      // to access unauthorized resources, log at info level. If false, this is either a request to determine\n   627→      // authorized operations or a filter (e.g for regex subscriptions) to filter out authorized resources.\n   628→      // In this case, log only at trace level.\n   629→      if (action.logIfDenied)\n   630→        authorizerLogger.info(logMessage)\n   631→      else\n   632→        authorizerLogger.trace(logMessage)\n   633→    }\n   634→  }\n   635→\n   636→  /**\n   637→    * Safely updates the resources ACLs by ensuring reads and writes respect the expected zookeeper version.\n   638→    * Continues to retry until it successfully updates zookeeper.\n   639→    *\n   640→    * Returns a boolean indicating if the content of the ACLs was actually changed.\n   641→    *\n   642→    * @param resource the resource to change ACLs for\n   643→    * @param getNewAcls function to transform existing acls to new ACLs\n   644→    * @return boolean indicating if a change was made\n   645→    */\n   646→  private def updateResourceAcls(resource: ResourcePattern)(getNewAcls: Set[AclEntry] => Set[AclEntry]): Boolean = {\n   647→    var currentVersionedAcls =\n   648→      if (aclCache.contains(resource))\n   649→        getAclsFromCache(resource)\n   650→      else\n   651→        getAclsFromZk(zkClient, resource)\n   652→    var newVersionedAcls: VersionedAcls = null\n   653→    var writeComplete = false\n [[kafka.security.authorizer.AclAuthorizer#createAcls]] while a delete is in\n   *   progress, these ACLs may or may not be considered for deletion depending on the order of updates.\n   *   The returned [[org.apache.kafka.server.authorizer.AclDeleteResult]] indicates which ACLs were deleted.</li>\n   *   <li>If the provided filters use resource pattern type\n   *   [[org.apache.kafka.common.resource.PatternType#MATCH]] that needs to filter all resources to determine\n   *   matching ACLs, only ACLs that have already been propagated to the broker processing the This may not include some ACLs that were persisted, but not yet propagated to all brokers. The\n   *   returned [[org.apache.kafka.server.authorizer.AclDeleteResult]] indicates which ACLs were deleted.</li>\n   *   <li>If the provided filters use other resource pattern types that perform a resourceBindingsBeingDeleted.getOrElseUpdate(binding, index)\n                }\n                matches\n              }\n            }\n            currentAcls -- aclsToRemove\n          }\n        } catch {\n          case e: Exception =>\n            resourceBindingsBeingDeleted.keys.foreach { binding =>\n              deleteExceptions.getOrElseUpdate(binding, apiException(e))\n            }\n deleteExceptions.get(binding).orNull) }\n    }\n    (0 until aclBindingFilters.size).map { i =>\n      new AclDeleteResult(deletedResult.getOrElse(i, Set.empty[AclBindingDeleteResult]).toSet.asJava)\n    }.map(CompletableFuture.completedFuture[AclDeleteResult]).asJava\n  }\n\n  override def acls(filter: AclBindingFilter): lang.Iterable[AclBinding] = {\n    val aclBindings = new AclOperation,\n                                       resourceType: ResourceType): AuthorizationResult = {\n    SecurityUtils.authorizeByResourceTypeCheckArgs(op, resourceType)\n\n    val principal = new KafkaPrincipal(\n      requestContext.principal().getPrincipalType,\n      requestContext.principal().getName)\n\n    if (isSuperUser(principal))\n      return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n\n    val resourceSnapshot = resourceCache\n    val principalStr = principal.toString\n    val host = requestContext.clientAddress().getHostAddress\n    val action = new Action(op, new ResourcePattern(resourceType, \"NONE\", PatternType.UNKNOWN), 0, true, true)\n\n    val denyLiterals = matchingResources(\n      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.DENY, resourceType, PatternType.LITERAL)\n\n    if (denyAll(denyLiterals)) {\n      logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = false)\n      return AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n    }\n\n    if (shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound) {\n      logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = true)\n      return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n    }\n\n    val denyPrefixes = matchingResources(\n      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.DENY, resourceType, PatternType.PREFIXED)\n\n    if (denyLiterals.isEmpty && denyPrefixes.isEmpty) {\n      if (hasMatchingResources(resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.PREFIXED)\n          || hasMatchingResources(resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.LITERAL)) {\n        logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = true)\n        return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n      } else {\n        logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = false)\n        return AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n      }\n    }\n\n    val allowLiterals = matchingResources(\n      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.LITERAL)\n    val allowPrefixes = matchingResources(\n      resourceSnapshot, principalStr, host, op, AclPermissionType.ALLOW, resourceType, PatternType.PREFIXED)\n\n    if (allowAny(allowLiterals, allowPrefixes, denyLiterals, denyPrefixes)) {\n      logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = true)\n      return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED\n    }\n\n    logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized = false)\n    AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n  }\n\n  private def matchingResources(resourceSnapshot: immutable.Map[ResourceTypeKey, immutable.Set[String]],\n                                principal: String, host: String, op: AclOperation, permission: AclPermissionType,\n                                resourceType: ResourceType, patternType: PatternType): ArrayBuffer[Set[String]] = {\n    val matched = ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]()\n    for (p <- Set(principal, AclEntry.WILDCARD_PRINCIPAL_STRING);\n         h <- Set(host, AclEntry.WILDCARD_HOST);\n         o <- Set(op, AclOperation.ALL)) {\n      val resourceTypeKey = ResourceTypeKey(\n        new AccessControlEntry(p, h, o, permission), resourceType, patternType)\n      resourceSnapshot.get(resourceTypeKey) match {\n        case Some(resources) => matched += resources\n        case None =>\n      }\n    }\n    matched\n  }\n\n  private def hasMatchingResources(resourceSnapshot: immutable.Map[ResourceTypeKey, immutable.Set[String]],\n                                   principal: String, host: String, op: AclOperation, permission: AclPermissionType,\n                                   resourceType: ResourceType, patternType: PatternType): Boolean = {\n    for (p <- Set(principal, AclEntry.WILDCARD_PRINCIPAL_STRING);\n         h <- Set(host, AclEntry.WILDCARD_HOST);\n         o <- Set(op, AclOperation.ALL)) {\n          val resourceTypeKey = ResourceTypeKey(\n            new AccessControlEntry(p, h, o, permission), resourceType, patternType)\n          if (resourceSnapshot.contains(resourceTypeKey))\n            return true\n    }\n    false\n  }\n\n  private def denyAll(denyLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean =\n    denyLiterals.exists(_.contains(ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE))\n\n\n  private def allowAny(allowLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]], allowPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]],\n                       denyLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]], denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n    (allowPrefixes.exists(_.exists(prefix => allowPrefix(prefix, denyPrefixes)))\n      || allowLiterals.exists(_.exists(literal => allowLiteral(literal, denyLiterals, denyPrefixes))))\n  }\n\n  private def allowLiteral(literalName: String, denyLiterals: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]],\n                           denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n    literalName match {\n      case ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE => true\n      case _ => !denyLiterals.exists(_.contains(literalName)) && !hasDominantPrefixedDeny(literalName, denyPrefixes)\n    }\n  }\n\n  private def allowPrefix(prefixName: String,\n                          denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n    !hasDominantPrefixedDeny(prefixName, denyPrefixes)\n  }\n\n  private def hasDominantPrefixedDeny(resourceName: String, denyPrefixes: ArrayBuffer[immutable.Set[String]]): Boolean = {\n    val sb = new StringBuilder\n    for (ch <- resourceName.toCharArray) {\n      sb.append(ch)\n      if (denyPrefixes.exists(p => p.contains(sb.toString()))) {\n        return true\n      }\n    }\n    false\n  }\n\n  private def authorizeAction(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext, action: Action): AuthorizationResult = {\n    val resource = action.resourcePattern\n    if (resource.patternType != PatternType.LITERAL) {\n      throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Only literal resources are supported. Got: \" + resource.patternType)\n    }\n\n    // ensure we compare identical classes\n    val sessionPrincipal = requestContext.principal\n    val principal = if (classOf[KafkaPrincipal] != sessionPrincipal.getClass)\n      new KafkaPrincipal(sessionPrincipal.getPrincipalType, sessionPrincipal.getName)\n    else\n      sessionPrincipal\n\n    val host = requestContext.clientAddress.getHostAddress\n    val operation = action.operation\n\n    def isEmptyAclAndAuthorized(acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n      if (acls.isEmpty) {\n        // No ACLs found for this resource, permission is determined by value of config allow.everyone.if.no.acl.found\n        authorizerLogger.debug(s\"No acl found for resource $resource, authorized = $shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound\")\n        shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound\n      } else false\n    }\n\n    def denyAclExists(acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n      // Check if there are any Deny ACLs which would forbid this operation.\n      matchingAclExists(operation, resource, principal, host, DENY, acls)\n    }\n\n    def allowAclExists(acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n      // Check if there are any Allow ACLs which would allow this operation.\n      // Allowing read, write, delete, or alter implies allowing describe.\n      // See #{org.apache.kafka.common.acl.AclOperation} for more details about ACL inheritance.\n      val allowOps = operation match {\n        case DESCRIBE => Set[AclOperation](DESCRIBE, READ, WRITE, DELETE, ALTER)\n        case DESCRIBE_CONFIGS => Set[AclOperation](DESCRIBE_CONFIGS, ALTER_CONFIGS)\n        case _ => Set[AclOperation](operation)\n      }\n      allowOps.exists(operation => matchingAclExists(operation, resource, principal, host, ALLOW, acls))\n    }\n\n    def aclsAllowAccess = {\n      // we allow an operation if no acls are found and user has configured to allow all users\n      // when no acls are found or if no deny acls are found and at least one allow acls matches.\n      val acls = matchingAcls(resource.resourceType, resource.name)\n      isEmptyAclAndAuthorized(acls) || (denyAclExists(acls) && allowAclExists(acls))\n    }\n\n    // Evaluate if operation is allowed\n    val authorized = isSuperUser(principal) || aclsAllowAccess\n\n    logAuditMessage(requestContext, action, authorized)\n    if (authorized) AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED else AuthorizationResult.DENIED\n  }\n\n  private def isSuperUser(principal: KafkaPrincipal): Boolean = {\n    if (superUsers.contains(principal)) {\n      authorizerLogger.debug(s\"principal = $principal is a super user, allowing operation without checking acls.\")\n      true\n    } else false\n  }\n\n  @nowarn(\"cat=deprecation\")\n  private def matchingAcls(resourceType: ResourceType, resourceName: String): AclSeqs = {\n    // this code is performance sensitive, make sure to run AclAuthorizerBenchmark after any changes\n\n    // save aclCache reference to a local val to get a consistent view of the cache during acl updates.\n    val aclCacheSnapshot = aclCache\n    val wildcard = aclCacheSnapshot.get(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE, PatternType.LITERAL))\n      .map(_.acls.toBuffer)\n      .getOrElse(mutable.Buffer.empty)\n\n    val literal = aclCacheSnapshot.get(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, resourceName, PatternType.LITERAL))\n      .map(_.acls.toBuffer)\n      .getOrElse(mutable.Buffer.empty)\n\n    val prefixed = new ArrayBuffer[AclEntry]\n    aclCacheSnapshot\n      .from(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, resourceName, PatternType.PREFIXED))\n      .to(new ResourcePattern(resourceType, resourceName.take(1), PatternType.PREFIXED))\n      .forKeyValue { (resource, acls) =>\n        if (resourceName.startsWith(resource.name)) prefixed ++= acls.acls\n      }\n\n    new AclSeqs(prefixed, wildcard, literal)\n  }\n\n  private def matchingAclExists(operation: AclOperation,\n                                resource: ResourcePattern,\n                                principal: KafkaPrincipal,\n                                host: String,\n                                permissionType: AclPermissionType,\n                                acls: AclSeqs): Boolean = {\n    acls.find { acl =>\n      acl.permissionType == permissionType &&\n        (acl.kafkaPrincipal == principal || acl.kafkaPrincipal == AclEntry.WILDCARD_PRINCIPAL) &&\n        (operation == acl.operation || acl.operation == AclOperation.ALL) &&\n        (acl.host == host || acl.host == AclEntry.WILDCARD_HOST)\n    }.exists { acl =>\n      authorizerLogger.debug(s\"operation = $operation on resource = $resource from host = $host is $permissionType based on acl = $acl\")\n      true\n    }\n  }\n\n  private def loadCache(): Unit = {\n    lock synchronized  {\n      loadAllAcls(zkClient, this, updateCache)\n    }\n  }\n\n  private[authorizer] def startZkChangeListeners(): Unit = {\n    aclChangeListeners = ZkAclChangeStore.stores\n      .map(store => store.createListener(AclChangedNotificationHandler, zkClient))\n  }\n\n  private def filterToResources(filter: ResourcePatternFilter): Set[ResourcePattern] = {\n    filter.patternType match {\n      case PatternType.LITERAL | PatternType.PREFIXED =>\n        Set(new ResourcePattern(filter.resourceType, filter.name, filter.patternType))\n      case PatternType.ANY =>\n        Set(new ResourcePattern(filter.resourceType, filter.name, PatternType.LITERAL),\n          new ResourcePattern(filter.resourceType, filter.name, PatternType.PREFIXED))\n      case _ => throw new IllegalArgumentException(s\"Cannot determine matching resources for patternType $filter\")\n    }\n  }\n\n  private def logAuditMessage(requestContext: AuthorizableRequestContext, action: Action, authorized: Boolean): Unit = {\n    def logMessage: String = {\n      val principal = requestContext.principal\n      val operation = SecurityUtils.operationName(action.operation)\n      val host = requestContext.clientAddress.getHostAddress\n      val resourceType = SecurityUtils.resourceTypeName(action.resourcePattern.resourceType)\n      val resource = s\"$resourceType$RESOURCE_SEPARATOR${action.resourcePattern.patternType}$RESOURCE_SEPARATOR${action.resourcePattern.name}\"\n      val authResult = if (authorized) \"Allowed\" else \"Denied\"\n      val apiKey = if (ApiKeys.hasId(requestContext.requestType)) ApiKeys.forId(requestContext.requestType).name else requestContext.requestType\n      val refCount = action.resourceReferenceCount\n\n      s\"Principal = $principal is $authResult Operation = $operation \" +\n        s\"from host = $host on resource = $resource for request = $apiKey with resourceRefCount = $refCount\"\n    }\n\n    if (authorized) {\n      // logIfAllowed is true if access is granted to the resource as a result of this authorization.\n      // In this case, log at debug level. If false, no access is actually granted, the result is used\n      // only to determine authorized operations. So log only at trace level.\n      if (action.logIfAllowed)\n        authorizerLogger.debug(logMessage)\n      else\n        authorizerLogger.trace(logMessage)\n    } else {\n      // logIfDenied is true if access to the resource was explicitly requested. Since this is an attempt\n      // to access unauthorized resources, log at info level. If false, this is either a request to determine\n      // authorized operations or a filter (e.g for regex subscriptions) to filter out authorized resources.\n      // In this case, log only at trace level.\n      if (action.logIfDenied)\n        authorizerLogger.info(logMessage)\n      else\n        authorizerLogger.trace(logMessage)\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n    * Safely updates the resources ACLs by ensuring reads and writes respect the expected zookeeper version.\n    * Continues to retry until it successfully updates zookeeper.\n    *\n    * Returns a boolean indicating if the content of the ACLs was actually changed.\n    *\n    * @param resource the resource to change ACLs for\n    * @param getNewAcls function to transform existing acls to new ACLs\n    * @return boolean indicating if a change was made\n    */\n  private def updateResourceAcls(resource: ResourcePattern)(getNewAcls: Set[AclEntry] => Set[AclEntry]): Boolean = {\n    var currentVersionedAcls =\n      if (aclCache.contains(resource))\n        getAclsFromCache(resource)\n      else\n        getAclsFromZk(zkClient, resource)\n    var newVersionedAcls: VersionedAcls = null\n    var writeComplete = false\n    var retries = 0\n    while (!writeComplete && retries <= maxUpdateRetries) {\n      val newAcls = getNewAcls(currentVersionedAcls.acls)\n      val (updateSucceeded, updateVersion) =\n        if (newAcls.nonEmpty) {\n          if (currentVersionedAcls.exists)\n            zkClient.conditionalSetAclsForResource(resource, newAcls, currentVersionedAcls.zkVersion)\n          else\n            zkClient.createAclsForResourceIfNotExists(resource, newAcls)\n        } else {\n          trace(s\"Deleting path for $resource because it had no ACLs remaining\")\n          (zkClient.conditionalDelete(resource, currentVersionedAcls.zkVersion), 0)\n        }\n\n      if (!updateSucceeded) {\n        trace(s\"Failed to update ACLs for $resource. Used version ${currentVersionedAcls.zkVersion}. Reading data and retrying update.\")\n        Thread.sleep(backoffTime)\n        currentVersionedAcls = getAclsFromZk(zkClient, resource)\n        retries += 1\n      } else {\n        newVersionedAcls = VersionedAcls(newAcls, updateVersion)\n        writeComplete = updateSucceeded\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (!writeComplete)\n      throw new IllegalStateException(s\"Failed to update ACLs for $resource after trying a maximum of $maxUpdateRetries times\")\n\n    if (newVersionedAcls.acls != currentVersionedAcls.acls) {\n      info(s\"Updated ACLs for $resource with new version ${newVersionedAcls.zkVersion}\")\n      debug(s\"Updated ACLs for $resource to $newVersionedAcls\")\n      updateCache(resource, newVersionedAcls)\n      updateAclChangedFlag(resource)\n      true\n    } else {\n      debug(s\"Updated ACLs for $resource, no change was made\")\n      updateCache(resource, newVersionedAcls) // Even if no change, update the version\n      false\n    }\n  }\n\n  private def getAclsFromCache(resource: ResourcePattern): VersionedAcls = {\n    aclCache.getOrElse(resource, throw new IllegalArgumentException(s\"ACLs do not exist in the cache for resource $resource\"))\n  }\n\n\n  // Visible for benchmark\n  def updateCache(resource: ResourcePattern, versionedAcls: VersionedAcls): Unit = {\n    val currentAces: Set[AccessControlEntry] = aclCache.get(resource).map(_.acls.map(_.ace)).getOrElse(Set.empty)\n    val newAces: Set[AccessControlEntry] = versionedAcls.acls.map(aclEntry => aclEntry.ace)\n    val acesToAdd = newAces.diff(currentAces)\n    val acesToRemove = currentAces.diff(newAces)\n\n    acesToAdd.foreach { ace =>\n      val resourceTypeKey = ResourceTypeKey(ace, resource.resourceType(), resource.patternType())\n      resourceCache.get(resourceTypeKey) match {\n        case Some(resources) => resourceCache += (resourceTypeKey -> (resources + resource.name()))\n        case None => resourceCache += (resourceTypeKey -> immutable.HashSet(resource.name()))\n      }\n    }\n    acesToRemove.foreach { ace =>\n      val resourceTypeKey = ResourceTypeKey(ace, resource.resourceType(), resource.patternType())\n      resourceCache.get(resourceTypeKey) match {\n        case Some(resources) =>\n          val newResources = resources - resource.name()\n          if (newResources.isEmpty) {\n            resourceCache -= resourceTypeKey\n          } else {\n            resourceCache += (resourceTypeKey -> newResources)\n          }\n        case None =>\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (versionedAcls.acls.nonEmpty) {\n      aclCache = aclCache.updated(resource, versionedAcls)\n    } else {\n      aclCache -= resource\n    }\n  }\n\n  private def Random.nextInt(retryBackoffJitterMs)\n  }\n\n  private def apiException(e: Throwable): ApiException = {\n    e match {\n      case e1: ApiException => e1\n      case e1 => new ApiException(e1)\n    }\n  }\n\n  private[authorizer] def processAclChangeNotification(resource: ResourcePattern): Unit = {\n    lock synchronized {\n      val versionedAcls = getAclsFromZk(zkClient, resource)\n      info(s\"Processing Acl change notification for $resource, versionedAcls : ${versionedAcls.acls}, zkVersion : ${versionedAcls.zkVersion}\")\n      updateCache(resource, versionedAcls)\n    }\n  }\n\n processAclChangeNotification(resource)\n    }\n  }\n\n  private case class ResourceTypeKey(ace: AccessControlEntry,\n                                     resourceType: ResourceType,\n
