specified for SASL mechanism \" + mechanism);\n   183→            if (!subjects.containsKey(mechanism))\n   184→                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Subject cannot be null for SASL mechanism \" + mechanism);\n   185→            LOG.trace(\"{} for mechanism={}: {}\", BrokerSecurityConfigs.CONNECTIONS_MAX_REAUTH_MS_CONFIG, mechanism,\n   186→                    connectionsMaxReauthMsByMechanism.get(mechanism));\n   187→        }\n   188→\n   189→        // Note that the old principal builder does not support SASL, so we do not need to pass the\n   190→        // authenticator or the transport layer\n   191→        this.principalBuilder = ChannelBuilders.createPrincipalBuilder(configs, kerberosNameParser, null);\n   192→\n   193→        saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize = (Integer) configs.get(BrokerSecurityConfigs.SASL_SERVER_MAX_RECEIVE_SIZE_CONFIG);\n   194→        if (saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize == null)\n   195→            saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize = BrokerSecurityConfigs.DEFAULT_SASL_SERVER_MAX_RECEIVE_SIZE;\n   196→    }\n   197→\n   198→    private void createSaslServer(String mechanism) throws IOException {\n   199→        this.saslMechanism = mechanism;\n   200→        Subject subject = subjects.get(mechanism);\n   201→        final AuthenticateCallbackHandler callbackHandler = callbackHandlers.get(mechanism);\n   202→        if (mechanism.equals(SaslConfigs.GSSAPI_MECHANISM)) {\n   203→            saslServer = createSaslKerberosServer(callbackHandler, configs, subject);\n   204→        } else {\n   205→            try {\n   206→                saslServer = Subject.doAs(subject, (PrivilegedExceptionAction<SaslServer>) () ->\n   207→                    Sasl.createSaslServer(saslMechanism, \"kafka\", serverAddress().getHostName(), configs, callbackHandler));\n   208→                if (saslServer == null) {\n   209→                    throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication with server mechanism \" + saslMechanism);\n   210→                }\n   211→            } catch (PrivilegedActionException e) {\n   212→                throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication with server mechanism \" + saslMechanism, e.getCause());\n   213→            }\n   214→        }\n   215→    }\n   216→\n   217→    private SaslServer createSaslKerberosServer(final AuthenticateCallbackHandler saslServerCallbackHandler, final Map<String, ?> configs, Subject subject) throws IOException {\n   218→        // server is using a JAAS-authenticated subject: determine service principal name and hostname from kafka server's subject.\n   219→        final String servicePrincipal = SaslClientAuthenticator.firstPrincipal(subject);\n   220→        KerberosName kerberosName;\n   221→        try {\n   222→            kerberosName = KerberosName.parse(servicePrincipal);\n   223→        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n   224→            throw new KafkaException(\"Principal has name with unexpected format \" + servicePrincipal);\n   225→        }\n   226→        final String servicePrincipalName = kerberosName.serviceName();\n   227→        final String serviceHostname = kerberosName.hostName();\n   228→\n   229→        LOG.debug(\"Creating SaslServer for {} with mechanism {}\", kerberosName, saslMechanism);\n   230→\n   231→        try {\n   232→            return Subject.doAs(subject, (PrivilegedExceptionAction<SaslServer>) () ->\n   233→                    Sasl.createSaslServer(saslMechanism, servicePrincipalName, serviceHostname, configs, saslServerCallbackHandler));\n   234→        } catch (PrivilegedActionException e) {\n   235→            throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication\", e.getCause());\n   236→        }\n   237→    }\n   238→\n   239→    /**\n   240→     * Evaluates client responses via `SaslServer.evaluateResponse` and returns the issued challenge to the client until\n   241→     * authentication succeeds or fails.\n   242→     *\n   243→     * The messages are sent and received as size delimited bytes that consists of a 4 byte network-ordered size N\n   244→     * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\n   245→     */\n   246→    @SuppressWarnings(\"fallthrough\")\n   247→    @Override\n   248→    public void authenticate() throws IOException {\n   249→        if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\n   250→            if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\n   251→                return;\n   252→\n   253→            if (saslServer != null && saslServer.isComplete()) {\n   254→                setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n   255→                return;\n   256→            }\n   257→\n   258→            // allocate on heap (as opposed to any socket server memory pool)\n   259→            if (netInBuffer == null) netInBuffer = new NetworkReceive(saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize, connectionId);\n   260→\n   261→            try {\n   262→                netInBuffer.readFrom(transportLayer);\n   263→            } catch (InvalidReceiveException e) {\n   264→                throw new SaslAuthenticationException(\"Failing SASL authentication due to invalid receive size\", e);\n   265→            }\n   266→            if (!netInBuffer.complete())\n   267→                return;\n   268→            netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n   269→        }\n   270→        byte[] clientToken = new byte[netInBuffer.payload().remaining()];\n   271→        netInBuffer.payload().get(clientToken, 0, clientToken.length);\n   272→        netInBuffer = null; // reset the networkReceive as we read all the data.\n   273→        try {\n   274→            switch (saslState) {\n   275→                case REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE:\n   276→                case HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST:\n   277→                case HANDSHAKE_REQUEST:\n   278→                    handleKafkaRequest(clientToken);\n   279→                    break;\n   280→                case REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM:\n   281→                    throw new SaslAuthenticationException(reauthInfo.badMechanismErrorMessage);\n   282→                case INITIAL_REQUEST:\n   283→                    if (handleKafkaRequest(clientToken))\n   284→                        break;\n   285→                    // For default GSSAPI, fall through to authenticate using the client token as the first GSSAPI packet.\n   286→                    // This is required for interoperability with 0.9.0.x clients which do not send handshake request\n   287→                case AUTHENTICATE:\n   288→                    handleSaslToken(clientToken);\n   289→                    // When the authentication exchange is complete and no more tokens are expected from the client,\n   290→                    // update SASL state. Current SASL state will be updated when outgoing writes to the client complete.\n   291→                    if (saslServer.isComplete())\n   292→                        setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n   293→                    break;\n   294→                default:\n   295→                    break;\n   296→            }\n   297→        } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n   298→            // Exception will be propagated after response is sent to client\n   299→            setSaslState(SaslState.FAILED, e);\n   300→        } catch (Exception e) {\n   301→            // In the case of IOExceptions and other unexpected exceptions, fail immediately\n   302→            saslState = SaslState.FAILED;\n   303→            LOG.debug(\"Failed during {}: {}\", reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText(), e.getMessage());\n   304→            throw e;\n   305→        }\n   306→    }\n   307→\n   308→    @Override\n   309→    public KafkaPrincipal principal() {\n   310→        Optional<SSLSession> sslSession = transportLayer instanceof SslTransportLayer ?\n   311→                Optional.of(((SslTransportLayer) transportLayer).sslSession()) : Optional.empty();\n   312→        SaslAuthenticationContext context = new SaslAuthenticationContext(saslServer, securityProtocol,\n   313→                clientAddress(), listenerName.value(), sslSession);\n   314→        KafkaPrincipal principal = principalBuilder.build(context);\n   315→        if (ScramMechanism.isScram(saslMechanism) && Boolean.parseBoolean((String) saslServer.getNegotiatedProperty(ScramLoginModule.TOKEN_AUTH_CONFIG))) {\n   316→            principal.tokenAuthenticated(true);\n   317→        }\n   318→        return principal;\n   319→    }\n   320→\n   321→    @Override\n   322→    public Optional<KafkaPrincipalSerde> principalSerde() {\n   323→        return principalBuilder instanceof KafkaPrincipalSerde ? Optional.of((KafkaPrincipalSerde) principalBuilder) : Optional.empty();\n   324→    }\n   325→\n   326→    @Override\n   327→    public boolean complete() {\n   328→        return saslState == SaslState.COMPLETE;\n   329→    }\n   330→\n   331→    @Override\n   332→    public void handleAuthenticationFailure() throws IOException {\n   333→        sendAuthenticationFailureResponse();\n   334→    }\n   335→\n   336→    @Override\n   337→    public void close() throws IOException {\n   338→        if (principalBuilder instanceof Closeable)\n   339→            Utils.closeQuietly((Closeable) principalBuilder, \"principal builder\");\n   340→        if (saslServer != null)\n   341→            saslServer.dispose();\n   342→    }\n   343→\n   344→    @Override\n   345→    public void reauthenticate(ReauthenticationContext reauthenticationContext) throws IOException {\n   346→        NetworkReceive saslHandshakeReceive = reauthenticationContext.networkReceive();\n   347→        if (saslHandshakeReceive == null)\n   348→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n   349→                    \"Invalid saslHandshakeReceive in server-side re-authentication context: null\");\n   350→        SaslServerAuthenticator previousSaslServerAuthenticator = (SaslServerAuthenticator) reauthenticationContext.previousAuthenticator();\n   351→        reauthInfo.reauthenticating(previousSaslServerAuthenticator.saslMechanism,\n   352→                previousSaslServerAuthenticator.principal(), reauthenticationContext.reauthenticationBeginNanos());\n   353→        previousSaslServerAuthenticator.close();\n   354→        netInBuffer = saslHandshakeReceive;\n   355→        LOG.debug(\"Beginning re-authentication: {}\", this);\n   356→        netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n   357→        setSaslState(SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE);\n   358→        authenticate();\n   359→    }\n   360→\n   361→    @Override\n   362→    public Long serverSessionExpirationTimeNanos() {\n   363→        return reauthInfo.sessionExpirationTimeNanos;\n   364→    }\n   365→\n   366→    @Override\n   367→    public Long reauthenticationLatencyMs() {\n   368→        return reauthInfo.reauthenticationLatencyMs();\n   369→    }\n   370→\n   371→    @Override\n   372→    public boolean connectedClientSupportsReauthentication() {\n   373→        return reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication;\n   374→    }\n   375→\n   376→    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState) {\n   377→        setSaslState(saslState, null);\n   378→    }\n   379→\n   380→    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState, AuthenticationException exception) {\n   381→        if (netOutBuffer != null && !netOutBuffer.completed()) {\n   382→            pendingSaslState = saslState;\n   383→            pendingException = exception;\n   384→        } else {\n   385→            this.saslState = saslState;\n   386→            LOG.debug(\"Set SASL server state to {} during {}\", saslState, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\n   387→            this.pendingSaslState = null;\n   388→            this.pendingException = null;\n   389→            if (exception != null)\n   390→                throw exception;\n   391→        }\n   392→    }\n   393→\n   394→    private boolean flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps() throws IOException {\n   395→        boolean flushedCompletely = flushNetOutBuffer();\n   396→        if (flushedCompletely) {\n   397→            transportLayer.removeInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n   398→            if (pendingSaslState != null)\n   399→                setSaslState(pendingSaslState, pendingException);\n   400→        } else\n   401→            transportLayer.addInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n   402→        return flushedCompletely;\n   403→    }\n   404→\n   405→    private boolean flushNetOutBuffer() throws IOException {\n   406→        if (!netOutBuffer.completed())\n   407→            netOutBuffer.writeTo(transportLayer);\n   408→        return netOutBuffer.completed();\n   409→    }\n   410→\n   411→    private InetAddress serverAddress() {\n   412→        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getLocalAddress();\n   413→    }\n   414→\n   415→    private InetAddress clientAddress() {\n   416→        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getInetAddress();\n   417→    }\n   418→\n   419→    private int clientPort() {\n   420→        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getPort();\n   421→    }\n   422→\n   423→    private void handleSaslToken(byte[] clientToken) throws IOException {\n   424→        if (!enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders) {\n   425→            byte[] response = saslServer.evaluateResponse(clientToken);\n   426→            if (saslServer.isComplete()) {\n   427→                reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n   428→                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating())\n   429→                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n   430→            }\n   431→            if (response != null) {\n   432→                netOutBuffer = ByteBufferSend.sizePrefixed(ByteBuffer.wrap(response));\n   433→                flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps();\n   434→            }\n   435→        } else {\n   436→            ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(clientToken);\n   437→            RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\n   438→            ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\n   439→            short version = header.apiVersion();\n   440→            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n   441→                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n   442→            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n   443→            if (apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_AUTHENTICATE) {\n   444→                IllegalSaslStateException e = new IllegalSaslStateException(\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \" + apiKey + \" during SASL authentication.\");\n   445→                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, requestAndSize.request.getErrorResponse(e));\n   446→                throw e;\n   447→            }\n   448→            if (!apiKey.isVersionSupported(version)) {\n   449→                // We cannot create an error response if the request version of SaslAuthenticate is not supported\n   450→                // This should not normally occur since clients typically check supported versions using ApiVersionsRequest\n   451→                throw new UnsupportedVersionException(\"Version \" + version + \" is not supported for apiKey \" + apiKey);\n   452→            }\n   453→            /*\n   454→             * The client sends multiple SASL_AUTHENTICATE requests, and the client is known\n   455→             * to support the required version if any one of them indicates it supports that\n   456→             * version.\n   457→             */\n   458→            if (!reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication)\n   459→                reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication = version > 0;\n   460→            SaslAuthenticateRequest saslAuthenticateRequest = (SaslAuthenticateRequest) requestAndSize.request;\n   461→\n   462→            try {\n   463→                byte[] responseToken = saslServer.evaluateResponse(\n   464→                        Utils.copyArray(saslAuthenticateRequest.data().authBytes()));\n   465→                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating() && saslServer.isComplete())\n   466→                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n   467→                // For versions with SASL_AUTHENTICATE header, send a response to SASL_AUTHENTICATE request even if token is empty.\n   468→                byte[] responseBytes = responseToken == null ? new byte[0] : responseToken;\n   469→                long sessionLifetimeMs = !saslServer.isComplete() ? 0L\n   470→                        : reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n   471→                sendKafkaResponse(requestContext, new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n   472→                        new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n   473→                        .setErrorCode(Errors.NONE.code())\n   474→                        .setAuthBytes(responseBytes)\n   475→                        .setSessionLifetimeMs(sessionLifetimeMs)));\n   476→            } catch (SaslAuthenticationException e) {\n   477→                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext,\n   478→                        new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n   479→                                new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n   480→                                .setErrorCode(Errors.SASL_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED.code())\n   481→                                .setErrorMessage(e.getMessage())));\n   482→                throw e;\n   483→            } catch (SaslException e) {\n   484→                KerberosError kerberosError = KerberosError.fromException(e);\n   485→                if (kerberosError != null && kerberosError.retriable()) {\n   486→                    // Handle retriable Kerberos exceptions as I/O exceptions rather than authentication exceptions\n   487→                    throw e;\n   488→                } else {\n   489→                    // DO NOT include error message from the `SaslException` in the client response since it may\n   490→                    // contain sensitive data like the existence of the user.\n   491→                    String errorMessage = \"Authentication failed during \"\n   492→                            + reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText()\n   493→                            + \" due to invalid credentials with SASL mechanism \" + saslMechanism;\n   494→                    buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n   495→                            new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n   496→                            .setErrorCode(Errors.SASL_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED.code())\n   497→                            .setErrorMessage(errorMessage)));\n   498→                    throw new SaslAuthenticationException(errorMessage, e);\n   499→                }\n   500→            }\n   501→        }\n   502→    }\n   503→\n   504→    private boolean handleKafkaRequest(byte[] requestBytes) throws IOException, AuthenticationException {\n   505→        boolean isKafkaRequest = false;\n   506→        String clientMechanism = null;\n   507→        try {\n   508→            ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(requestBytes);\n   509→            RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\n   510→            ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\n   511→\n   512→            // A valid Kafka request header was received. SASL authentication tokens are now expected only\n   513→            // following a SaslHandshakeRequest since this is not a GSSAPI client token from a Kafka 0.9.0.x client.\n   514→            if (saslState == SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST)\n   515→                setSaslState(SaslState.HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST);\n   516→            isKafkaRequest = true;\n   517→\n   518→            // Raise an error prior to parsing if the api cannot be handled at this layer. This avoids\n   519→            // unnecessary exposure to some of the more complex schema types.\n   520→            if (apiKey != ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS && apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_HANDSHAKE)\n   521→                throw new IllegalSaslStateException(\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \" + apiKey + \" during SASL handshake.\");\n   522→\n   523→            LOG.debug(\"Handling Kafka request {} during {}\", apiKey, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\n   524→\n   525→\n   526→            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n   527→                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n   528→            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n   529→            if (apiKey == ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS)\n   530→                handleApiVersionsRequest(requestContext, (ApiVersionsRequest) requestAndSize.request);\n   531→            else\n   532→                clientMechanism = handleHandshakeRequest(requestContext, (SaslHandshakeRequest) requestAndSize.request);\n   533→        } catch (InvalidRequestException e) {\n   534→            if (saslState == SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST) {\n   535→                // InvalidRequestException is thrown if the request is not in Kafka format or if the API key\n   536→                // is invalid. For compatibility with 0.9.0.x where the first packet is a GSSAPI token\n   537→                // starting with 0x60, revert to GSSAPI for both these exceptions.\n   538→                if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\n   539→                    StringBuilder tokenBuilder = new StringBuilder();\n   540→                    for (byte b : requestBytes) {\n   541→                        tokenBuilder.append(String.format(\"%02x\", b));\n   542→                        if (tokenBuilder.length() >= 20)\n   543→                             break;\n   544→                    }\n   545→                    LOG.debug(\"Received client packet of length {} starting with bytes 0x{}, process as GSSAPI packet\", requestBytes.length, tokenBuilder);\n   546→                }\n   547→                if (enabledMechanisms.contains(SaslConfigs.GSSAPI_MECHANISM)) {\n   548→                    LOG.debug(\"First client packet is not a SASL mechanism request, using default mechanism GSSAPI\");\n   549→                    clientMechanism = SaslConfigs.GSSAPI_MECHANISM;\n   550→                } else\n   551→                    throw new UnsupportedSaslMechanismException(\"Exception handling first SASL packet from client, GSSAPI is not supported by server\", e);\n   552→            } else\n   553→                throw e;\n   554→        }\n   555→        if (clientMechanism != null && (!reauthInfo.reauthenticating()\n   556→                || reauthInfo.saslMechanismUnchanged(clientMechanism))) {\n   557→            createSaslServer(clientMechanism);\n   558→            setSaslState(SaslState.AUTHENTICATE);\n   559→        }\n   560→        return isKafkaRequest;\n   561→    }\n   562→\n   563→    private String handleHandshakeRequest(RequestContext context, SaslHandshakeRequest handshakeRequest) throws IOException, UnsupportedSaslMechanismException {\n   564→        String clientMechanism = handshakeRequest.data().mechanism();\n   565→        short version = context.header.apiVersion();\n   566→        if (version >= 1)\n   567→            this.enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders(true);\n   568→        if (enabledMechanisms.contains(clientMechanism)) {\n   569→            LOG.debug(\"Using SASL mechanism '{}' provided by client\", clientMechanism);\n   570→            sendKafkaResponse(context, new SaslHandshakeResponse(\n   571→                    new SaslHandshakeResponseData().setErrorCode(Errors.NONE.code()).setMechanisms(enabledMechanisms)));\n   572→            return clientMechanism;\n   573→        } else {\n   574→            LOG.debug(\"SASL mechanism '{}' requested by client is not supported\", clientMechanism);\n   575→            buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(context, new SaslHandshakeResponse(\n   576→                    new SaslHandshakeResponseData().setErrorCode(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_SASL_MECHANISM.code()).setMechanisms(enabledMechanisms)));\n   577→            throw new UnsupportedSaslMechanismException(\"Unsupported SASL mechanism \" + clientMechanism);\n   578→        }\n   579→    }\n   580→\n   581→    // Visible to override for testing\n   582→    protected void enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders(boolean flag) {\n   583→        this.enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders = flag;\n   584→    }\n   585→\n   586→    private void handleApiVersionsRequest(RequestContext context, ApiVersionsRequest apiVersionsRequest) throws IOException {\n   587→        if (saslState != SaslState.HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST)\n   588→            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Unexpected ApiVersions request received during SASL authentication state \" + saslState);\n   589→\n   590→        if (apiVersionsRequest.hasUnsupportedRequestVersion())\n   591→            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionsRequest.getErrorResponse(0, Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION.exception()));\n   592→        else if (!apiVersionsRequest.isValid())\n   593→            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionsRequest.getErrorResponse(0, Errors.INVALID_REQUEST.exception()));\n   594→        else {\n   595→            metadataRegistry.registerClientInformation(new ClientInformation(apiVersionsRequest.data().clientSoftwareName(),\n   596→                apiVersionsRequest.data().clientSoftwareVersion()));\n   597→            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionSupplier.get());\n   598→            setSaslState(SaslState.HANDSHAKE_REQUEST);\n   599→        }\n   600→    }\n   601→\n   602→    /**\n   603→     * Build a {@link Send} response on {@link #authenticate()} failure. The actual response is sent out when\n   604→     * {@link #sendAuthenticationFailureResponse()} is called.\n   605→     */\n   606→    private void buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(RequestContext context, AbstractResponse response) {\n   607→        authenticationFailureSend = context.buildResponseSend(response);\n   608→    }\n   609→\n   610→    /**\n   611→     * Send any authentication failure response that may have been previously built.\n   612→     */\n   613→    private void sendAuthenticationFailureResponse() throws IOException {\n   614→        if (authenticationFailureSend == null)\n   615→            return;\n   616→        sendKafkaResponse(authenticationFailureSend);\n   617→        authenticationFailureSend = null;\n   618→    }\n   619→\n   620→    private void sendKafkaResponse(RequestContext context, AbstractResponse response) throws IOException {\n   621→        sendKafkaResponse(context.buildResponseSend(response));\n   622→    }\n   623→\n   624→    private void sendKafkaResponse(Send send) throws IOException {\n   625→        netOutBuffer = send;\n   626→        flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps();\n   627→    }\n   628→\n   629→    /**\n   630→     * Information related to re-authentication\n   631→     */\n   632→    private class ReauthInfo {\n   633→        public String previousSaslMechanism;\n   634→        public KafkaPrincipal previousKafkaPrincipal;\n   635→        public long reauthenticationBeginNanos;\n   636→        public Long sessionExpirationTimeNanos;\n   637→        public boolean connectedClientSupportsReauthentication;\n   638→        public long authenticationEndNanos;\n   639→        public String badMechanismErrorMessage;\n   640→\n   641→        public void reauthenticating(String previousSaslMechanism, KafkaPrincipal previousKafkaPrincipal,\n   642→                long reauthenticationBeginNanos) {\n   643→            this.previousSaslMechanism = Objects.requireNonNull(previousSaslMechanism);\n   644→            this.previousKafkaPrincipal = Objects.requireNonNull(previousKafkaPrincipal);\n   645→            this.reauthenticationBeginNanos = reauthenticationBeginNanos;\n   646→        }\n   647→\n   648→        public boolean reauthenticating() {\n   649→            return previousSaslMechanism != null;\n   650→        }\n   651→\n   652→        public String authenticationOrReauthenticationText() {\n   653→            return reauthenticating() ? \"re-authentication\" : \"authentication\";\n   654→        }\n   655→\n   656→        public void ensurePrincipalUnchanged(KafkaPrincipal reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal) throws SaslAuthenticationException {\n   657→            if (!previousKafkaPrincipal.equals(reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal)) {\n   658→                throw new SaslAuthenticationException(String.format(\n   659→                        \"Cannot change principals during re-authentication from %s.%s: %s.%s\",\n   660→                        previousKafkaPrincipal.getPrincipalType(), previousKafkaPrincipal.getName(),\n   661→                        reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal.getPrincipalType(), reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal.getName()));\n   662→            }\n   663→        }\n   664→\n   665→        /*\n   666→         * We define the REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM state because the failed re-authentication\n   667→         * metric does not get updated if we send back an error immediately upon the\n   668→         * start of retvalSessionLifetimeMs);\n   708→            } else {\n   709→                if (sessionExpirationTimeNanos != null)\n   710→                    LOG.debug(\n   711→ 726→            long latencyNanos = authenticationEndNanos - reauthenticationBeginNanos;\n   727→            return latencyNanos == 0L ? 0L : Math.max(1L, Math.round(latencyNanos / 1000.0 / 1000.0));\n   728→        }\n   729→\n   730→        private long zeroIfNegative(long value) {\n   731→            return Math.max(0L, value);\n   732→        }        \n   733→    }\n   734→}\n /**\n     * The internal state transitions for initial authentication of a channel on the\n     * server side are declared in order, starting with {@link #INITIAL_REQUEST} and\n     * ending in either {@link #COMPLETE} or {@link #FAILED}.\n     * <p>\n     * Re-authentication of a channel on the server side starts with the state\n     * {@link #REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE}. It may then flow to\n     * {@link #REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM} before a transition to {@link #FAILED} if\n     * re-authentication is attempted with a mechanism different than the original\n     * one; otherwise it joins the authentication flow at the {@link #AUTHENTICATE}\n     * state and likewise ends at either {@link #COMPLETE} or {@link #FAILED}.\n     */\n    private enum SaslState {\n        INITIAL_REQUEST,               // May be GSSAPI token, SaslHandshake or ApiVersions for authentication\n        HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST, // May be SaslHandshake or ApiVersions\n        HANDSHAKE_REQUEST,             // After an ApiVersions request, next request must be SaslHandshake\n        AUTHENTICATE,                  // Authentication tokens (SaslHandshake v1 and above indicate SaslAuthenticate headers)\n        COMPLETE,                      // Authentication completed successfully\n        FAILED,                        // Authentication failed\n        REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE,      // Initial state for re-authentication, processes SASL handshake request\n        REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM,          // When re-authentication requested with wrong mechanism, generate exception\n    }\n\n    private final SecurityProtocol securityProtocol;\n    private final ListenerName listenerName;\n    private final String connectionId;\n    private final private final Time time;\n    private final ReauthInfo reauthInfo;\n    private final ChannelMetadataRegistry metadataRegistry;\n    private final Supplier<ApiVersionsResponse> apiVersionSupplier;\n\n    // Current SASL state\n    private SaslState saslState = SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST;\n    // Next SASL state to be set when outgoing writes associated with the current SASL state complete\n pendingException = null;\n    private SaslServer saslServer;\n    private String saslMechanism;\n\n    // buffers used in `authenticate`\n    private Integer saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize;\n               TransportLayer transportLayer,\n                                   Map<String, Long> connectionsMaxReauthMsByMechanism,\n                                   ChannelMetadataRegistry IllegalArgumentException(\"Callback handler not specified for SASL mechanism \" + mechanism);\n            if (!subjects.containsKey(mechanism))\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Subject cannot be null for SASL mechanism \" + mechanism);\n            LOG.trace(\"{} for mechanism={}: {}\", BrokerSecurityConfigs.CONNECTIONS_MAX_REAUTH_MS_CONFIG, subject = subjects.get(mechanism);\n        final AuthenticateCallbackHandler callbackHandler = callbackHandlers.get(mechanism);\n        if (mechanism.equals(SaslConfigs.GSSAPI_MECHANISM)) {\n            saslServer = createSaslKerberosServer(callbackHandler, configs, subject);\n        } else {\n            try {\n                saslServer = Subject.doAs(subject, (PrivilegedExceptionAction<SaslServer>) () ->\n                    Sasl.createSaslServer(saslMechanism, \"kafka\", serverAddress().getHostName(), configs, callbackHandler));\n                if (saslServer == null) {\n                    throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication with server mechanism \" + saslMechanism);\n                }\n            } catch (PrivilegedActionException e) {\n                throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication with server mechanism \" + saslMechanism, e.getCause());\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private SaslServer createSaslKerberosServer(final AuthenticateCallbackHandler saslServerCallbackHandler, final Map<String, ?> configs, Subject subject) throws IOException {\n        // server is using a JAAS-authenticated subject: determine service principal name and hostname from kafka server's subject.\n        final String servicePrincipal = SaslClientAuthenticator.firstPrincipal(subject);\n        KerberosName kerberosName;\n        try {\n            kerberosName = KerberosName.parse(servicePrincipal);\n        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n            throw new KafkaException(\"Principal has name with unexpected format \" + servicePrincipal);\n        }\n        final String servicePrincipalName = kerberosName.serviceName();\n        final String serviceHostname = kerberosName.hostName();\n\n        LOG.debug(\"Creating SaslServer for {} with mechanism {}\", kerberosName, saslMechanism);\n\n        try {\n            return Subject.doAs(subject, (PrivilegedExceptionAction<SaslServer>) () ->\n                    Sasl.createSaslServer(saslMechanism, servicePrincipalName, serviceHostname, configs, saslServerCallbackHandler));\n        } catch (PrivilegedActionException e) {\n            throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication\", e.getCause());\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Evaluates client responses via `SaslServer.evaluateResponse` and returns the issued challenge to the client until\n     * authentication succeeds or fails.\n     *\n     * The messages are sent and received as size delimited bytes that consists of a 4 byte network-ordered size N\n     * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\n     */\n    @SuppressWarnings(\"fallthrough\")\n    @Override\n    public void authenticate() throws IOException {\n        if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\n            if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\n                return;\n\n            if (saslServer != null && saslServer.isComplete()) {\n                setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // allocate on heap (as opposed to any socket server memory pool)\n            if (netInBuffer == null) netInBuffer = new NetworkReceive(saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize, connectionId);\n\n            try {\n                netInBuffer.readFrom(transportLayer);\n            } catch (InvalidReceiveException e) {\n                throw new SaslAuthenticationException(\"Failing SASL authentication due to invalid receive size\", e);\n            }\n            if (!netInBuffer.complete())\n                return;\n            netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n        }\n        byte[] clientToken = new byte[netInBuffer.payload().remaining()];\n        netInBuffer.payload().get(clientToken, 0, clientToken.length);\n        netInBuffer = null; // reset the networkReceive as we read all the data.\n        try {\n            switch (saslState) {\n                case REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE:\n                case HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST:\n                case HANDSHAKE_REQUEST:\n                    handleKafkaRequest(clientToken);\n                    break;\n                case REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM:\n                    throw new SaslAuthenticationException(reauthInfo.badMechanismErrorMessage);\n                case INITIAL_REQUEST:\n                    if (handleKafkaRequest(clientToken))\n                        break;\n                    // For default GSSAPI, fall through to authenticate using the client token as the first GSSAPI packet.\n                    // This is required for interoperability with 0.9.0.x clients which do not send handshake request\n                case AUTHENTICATE:\n                    handleSaslToken(clientToken);\n                    // When the authentication exchange is complete and no more tokens are expected from the client,\n                    // update SASL state. Current SASL state will be updated when outgoing writes to the client complete.\n                    if (saslServer.isComplete())\n                        setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n                    break;\n                default:\n                    break;\n            }\n        } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n            // Exception will be propagated after response is sent to client\n            setSaslState(SaslState.FAILED, e);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            // In the case of IOExceptions and other unexpected exceptions, fail immediately\n            saslState = SaslState.FAILED;\n            LOG.debug(\"Failed during {}: {}\", reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText(), e.getMessage());\n            throw e;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaPrincipal principal() {\n        Optional<SSLSession> sslSession = transportLayer instanceof SslTransportLayer ?\n                Optional.of(((SslTransportLayer) transportLayer).sslSession()) : Optional.empty();\n        SaslAuthenticationContext context = new SaslAuthenticationContext(saslServer, securityProtocol,\n                clientAddress(), listenerName.value(), sslSession);\n        KafkaPrincipal principal = principalBuilder.build(context);\n        if (ScramMechanism.isScram(saslMechanism) && Boolean.parseBoolean((String) saslServer.getNegotiatedProperty(ScramLoginModule.TOKEN_AUTH_CONFIG))) {\n            principal.tokenAuthenticated(true);\n        }\n        return principal;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Optional<KafkaPrincipalSerde> principalSerde() {\n        return principalBuilder instanceof KafkaPrincipalSerde ? Optional.of((KafkaPrincipalSerde) principalBuilder) : Optional.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean complete() {\n        return saslState == SaslState.COMPLETE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void handleAuthenticationFailure() throws IOException {\n        sendAuthenticationFailureResponse();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void close() throws IOException {\n        if (principalBuilder instanceof Closeable)\n            Utils.closeQuietly((Closeable) principalBuilder, \"principal builder\");\n        if (saslServer != null)\n            saslServer.dispose();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void reauthenticate(ReauthenticationContext reauthenticationContext) throws IOException {\n        NetworkReceive saslHandshakeReceive = reauthenticationContext.networkReceive();\n        if (saslHandshakeReceive == null)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n                    \"Invalid saslHandshakeReceive in server-side re-authentication context: null\");\n        SaslServerAuthenticator previousSaslServerAuthenticator = (SaslServerAuthenticator) reauthenticationContext.previousAuthenticator();\n        reauthInfo.reauthenticating(previousSaslServerAuthenticator.saslMechanism,\n                previousSaslServerAuthenticator.principal(), reauthenticationContext.reauthenticationBeginNanos());\n        previousSaslServerAuthenticator.close();\n        netInBuffer = saslHandshakeReceive;\n        LOG.debug(\"Beginning re-authentication: {}\", this);\n        netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n        setSaslState(SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE);\n        authenticate();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Long serverSessionExpirationTimeNanos() {\n        return reauthInfo.sessionExpirationTimeNanos;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Long reauthenticationLatencyMs() {\n        return reauthInfo.reauthenticationLatencyMs();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean connectedClientSupportsReauthentication() {\n        return reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication;\n    }\n\n    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState) {\n        setSaslState(saslState, null);\n    }\n\n    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState, AuthenticationException exception) {\n        if (netOutBuffer != null && !netOutBuffer.completed()) {\n            pendingSaslState = saslState;\n            pendingException = exception;\n        } else {\n            this.saslState = saslState;\n            LOG.debug(\"Set SASL server state to {} during {}\", saslState, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\n            this.pendingSaslState = null;\n            this.pendingException = null;\n            if (exception != null)\n                throw exception;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private boolean flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps() throws IOException {\n        boolean flushedCompletely = flushNetOutBuffer();\n        if (flushedCompletely) {\n            transportLayer.removeInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n            if (pendingSaslState != null)\n                setSaslState(pendingSaslState, pendingException);\n        } else\n            transportLayer.addInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n        return flushedCompletely;\n    }\n\n    private boolean flushNetOutBuffer() throws IOException {\n        if (!netOutBuffer.completed())\n            netOutBuffer.writeTo(transportLayer);\n        return netOutBuffer.completed();\n    }\n\n    private InetAddress serverAddress() {\n        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getLocalAddress();\n    }\n\n    private InetAddress clientAddress() {\n        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getInetAddress();\n    }\n\n    private int clientPort() {\n        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getPort();\n    }\n\n    private void handleSaslToken(byte[] clientToken) throws IOException {\n        if (!enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders) {\n            byte[] response = saslServer.evaluateResponse(clientToken);\n            if (saslServer.isComplete()) {\n                reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating())\n                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n            }\n            if (response != null) {\n                netOutBuffer = ByteBufferSend.sizePrefixed(ByteBuffer.wrap(response));\n                flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps();\n            }\n        } else {\n            ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(clientToken);\n            RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\n            ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\n            short version = header.apiVersion();\n            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n            if (apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_AUTHENTICATE) {\n                IllegalSaslStateException e = new IllegalSaslStateException(\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \" + apiKey + \" during SASL authentication.\");\n                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, requestAndSize.request.getErrorResponse(e));\n                throw e;\n            }\n            if (!apiKey.isVersionSupported(version)) {\n                // We cannot create an error response if the request version of SaslAuthenticate is not supported\n                // This should not normally occur since clients typically check supported versions using ApiVersionsRequest\n                throw new UnsupportedVersionException(\"Version \" + version + \" is not supported for apiKey \" + apiKey);\n            }\n            /*\n             * The client sends multiple SASL_AUTHENTICATE requests, and the client is known\n             * to support the required version if any one of them indicates it supports that\n             * version.\n             */\n            if (!reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication)\n                reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication = version > 0;\n            SaslAuthenticateRequest saslAuthenticateRequest = (SaslAuthenticateRequest) requestAndSize.request;\n\n            try {\n                byte[] responseToken = saslServer.evaluateResponse(\n                        Utils.copyArray(saslAuthenticateRequest.data().authBytes()));\n                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating() && saslServer.isComplete())\n                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n                // For versions with SASL_AUTHENTICATE header, send a response to SASL_AUTHENTICATE request even if token is empty.\n                byte[] responseBytes = responseToken == null ? new byte[0] : responseToken;\n                long sessionLifetimeMs = !saslServer.isComplete() ? 0L\n                        : reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n                sendKafkaResponse(requestContext, new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n
